The fiesta was an effective medium to give the Ryanites an exposure to the world of \u2018Fun and Frolic\u2019. The entire school was decorated with buntings and the entire school staff participated in the carnival. There were fun filled games Children were amused by the various games like Lucky Seven, Lucky Key, Ring the Duckling, Hoopla and many more. All the winners were suitably re', ...', warded. The fiesta highlighted visionary Chairman Sir Dr. A.F.Pinto\u2019s motto of creating a balance between education and co-curricular activities to provide the Ryanites an opportunity for holistic development.
